def iot(self, node):
    res = []
    if node.lef:
        res += self.iot(node.lef)
    
    res.append(node.value)
    
    if node.right:
        res += self.iot(node.right)
    
    return res

def in_order_traversal(self):
    res += self.iot(self.root.left)
    res.append(root.value)
    res += self.iot(root.right) ^loZ5q0kf

# PRE
def pot(self, node):
    res = []

    res.append(node.value)

    if node.lef:
        res += self.pot(node.lef)
    
    if node.right:
        res += self.pot(node.right)
    
    return res
 ^VM8SnoCK

# Post
def post(self, node):
    res = []

    if node.lef:
        res += self.post(node.lef)
    
    if node.right:
        res += self.post(node.right)

    res.append(node.value)
    
    return res ^9OXG0Qy8

# DFS
def dfs(node)
    res = []
    stack = [node]
    while stack:
        cu = stack.pop()
        res.append(cu.value)
        if cu.right:
            stack.append(cu.right)
        if cu.left:
            stack.append(cu.left)
    return res ^ZgNc22BW

# BFS
def bfs(node)
    res = []
    queue = [node]
    while queue:
        cu = queue.pop(0)
        res.append(cu.value)
        if cu.left:
            queue.append(cu.left)
        if cu.right:
            queue.append(cu.right)
    return res
     ^iqLmSgR0
